(src)="80014"> Layal Mounir Abboud ( Arabic : ليال عبود‎‎:[layāl ˈabˈboud ] ; born 15 May 1982 ) is a Lebanese pop singer , folk music entertainer , sound-lyric poet , concert dancer , fit model , Muslim humanitarian and businesswoman.[1][2][3 ]
(trg)="86"> Layal Mounir Abboud ( Arabic : ليال عبود ‎ ‎ : [ layāl ˈabˈboud ] ; born 15 May 1982 ) He kanaka meleʻo Lebanona , he mea hoʻokani pila , he mele mele , he hula hula , he kūpono , he kanaka aloha Muslim a he wahine kālepa . [ 1 ] [ 2 ] [ 3 ]

(trg)="92"> Discography
(src)="80022"> Rhino Bucket is a hard rock band from Van Nuys , Los Angeles , California .
(trg)="93"> Rhino Bucket is a hard rock band from Van Nuys , Los Angeles , California .
(src)="80023"> The band was formed in February 1988 by Georg Dolivo ( lead vocals , rhythm guitar ) , Reeve Downes ( bass guitar , backing vocals ) and Greg Fields ( lead guitar , backing vocals ) .
(src)="80024"> [ 1 ] This lineup played the Los Angeles rock scene for a year with contemporaries such as Junkyard and The Four Horsemen .
(src)="80025"> Warner Brothers signed the band in 1989 and they released their self-titled debut album in 1990 with Liam Jason from Warrior on drums .
(trg)="94"> The band was formed in February 1988 by Georg Dolivo ( lead vocals , rhythm guitar ) , Reeve Downes ( bass guitar , backing vocals ) and Greg Fields ( lead guitar , backing vocals ) .
(trg)="95"> [ 1 ] This lineup played the Los Angeles rock scene for a year with contemporaries such as Junkyard and The Four Horsemen .
(trg)="96"> Warner Brothers signed the band in 1989 and they released their self-titled debut album in 1990 with Liam Jason from Warrior on drums .
(src)="80026"> Their second album , 1992 's Get Used To It , was written and recorded in Memphis with producer Terry Manning .
(src)="80027"> The album contained " Ride With Yourself " which was featured in the hit movie and multi platinum soundtrack Wayne 's World .
(src)="80028"> In 1993 , drummer Simon Wright ( AC/DC , Dio ) joined the band and appeared on the 1994 album Pain .
(src)="80029"> The band continued extensive touring , but by 1996 the band went on what turned out to be an extended hiatus .
(trg)="97"> Their second album , 1992 ' s Get Used To It , was written and recorded in Memphis with producer Terry Manning .
(trg)="98"> The album contained " Ride With Yourself " which was featured in the hit movie and multi platinum soundtrack Wayne ' s World .
(trg)="99"> In 1993 , drummer Simon Wright ( AC / DC , Dio ) joined the band and appeared on the 1994 album Pain .
(trg)="100"> The band continued extensive touring , but by 1996 the band went on what turned out to be an extended hiatus .
(src)="80030"> Rhino Bucket reformed in 2001 with Brian " Damage " Forsythe from Kix joining the original lineup of Dolivo , Downes and Enx on lead guitar replacing the departing Fields ( aka Fidelman ) who had gone on to a successful producing and engineering career .
(src)="80031"> The band worked on a few movie soundtracks including the pot cult film Rolling Kansas and the title song for the movie The Outdoorsmen - Blood , Sweat & Beers .
(src)="80032"> Again the band became a fixture on a now quite different L.A. rock scene .
(trg)="101"> Rhino Bucket reformed in 2001 with Brian " Damage " Forsythe from Kix joining the original lineup of Dolivo , Downes and Enx on lead guitar replacing the departing Fields ( aka Fidelman ) who had gone on to a successful producing and engineering career .
(trg)="102"> The band worked on a few movie soundtracks including the pot cult film Rolling Kansas and the title song for the movie The Outdoorsmen - Blood , Sweat & Beers .
(trg)="103"> Again the band became a fixture on a now quite different L.A. rock scene .
(src)="80033"> In April 2006 Rhino Bucket released And Then It Got Ugly and then proceeded to tour with like minded friends Broken Teeth , Supersuckers and Kix .
(src)="80034"> 2007 saw the release of two new CDs Pain & Suffering and No Song Left Behind .
(src)="80035"> The former is an enhanced ( 5 new tracks ) of their 1994 album Pain , while the latter is a compilation of unreleased songs and live performances .
(src)="80036"> In July of the same year Simon Wright reunited with the band at the Rocklahoma festival .
(src)="80037"> Rhino Bucket released The Hardest Town in May 2009 with Wright behind the kit .
(src)="80038"> The band was also featured on The Wrestler soundtrack[2 ] and album during this time .
(src)="80039"> In 2010 the band returned to Europe for the first time in over 15 years with a 45 date tour that travelled to 14 countries .

(src)="80040"> Rhino Bucket released their sixth studio album Who 's Got Mine ? in January 2011 to enthusiastic reviews by both press and fans .
(src)="80041"> The band then embarked on two European tours making 83 appearances most notably at the Sweden Rock Festival where they played for over 10,000 fans .
(src)="80042"> A 51 show American tour followed in the Summer and Fall .
(trg)="111"> Rhino Bucket released their sixth studio album Who ' s Got Mine ? in January 2011 to enthusiastic reviews by both press and fans .
(trg)="112"> The band then embarked on two European tours making 83 appearances most notably at the Sweden Rock Festival where they played for over 10,000 fans .

(src)="80043"> Rhino Bucket continues to tour .
(src)="80044"> In 2014 , they completed 200 shows in Europe and North America in support of a live album entitled " Sunrise on Sunset " ( 2013 ) .
(src)="80045"> The band is currently playing select dates in America , such as the M3 Festival in Baltimore , and also some of the Monsters of Rock Cruises ( 2012 , 2015 , 2016 , planned 2018[3 ] ) .
(src)="80046"> Rhino Bucket will start a 30 date European tour January 4th in Verviers , Belgium .

(trg)="146"> Retrieved 17 March 2018 .. mw-parser-output cite.citation { font-style : inherit } .mw-parser-output q { quotes : " \ " " " \ " " " ' " " ' " } .mw-parser-output code.cs1-code { color : inherit ; background : inherit ; border : inherit ; padding : inherit } .mw-parser-output .cs1-lock-free a { background : url ( " / / upload.wikimedia.org / wikipedia / commons / thumb / 6 / 65 / Lock-green.svg / 9px-Lock-green.svg.png " ) no-repeat ; background-position : right .1em center } .mw-parser-output .cs1-lock-limited a , .mw-parser-output .cs1-lock-registration a { background : url ( " / / upload.wikimedia.org / wikipedia / commons / thumb / d / d6 / Lock-gray-alt-2.svg / 9px-Lock-gray-alt-2.svg.png " ) no-repeat ; background-position : right .1em center } .mw-parser-output .cs1-lock-subscription a { background : url ( " / / upload.wikimedia.org / wikipedia / commons / thumb / a / aa / Lock-red-alt-2.svg / 9px-Lock-red-alt-2.svg.png " ) no-repeat ; background-position : right .1em center } .mw-parser-output .cs1-subscription , .mw-parser-output .cs1-registration { color : # 555 } .mw-parser-output .cs1-subscription span , .mw-parser-output .cs1-registration span { border-bottom : 1px dotted ; cursor : help } .mw-parser-output .cs1-hidden-error { display : none ; font-size : 100 % } .mw-parser-output .cs1-visible-error { font-size : 100 % } .mw-parser-output .cs1-subscription , .mw-parser-output .cs1-registration , .mw-parser-output .cs1-format { font-size : 95 % } .mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-left , .mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-wl-left { padding-left : 0.2em } .mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-right , .mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-wl-right { padding-right : 0.2em }
(src)="80088"> Rankin/Bass Productions , Inc. ( founded as Videocraft International , Ltd. and later known as Rankin/Bass Animated Entertainment ) was an American production company , known for its seasonal television specials , particularly its work in stop motion animation .
(src)="80089"> Rankin/Bass stop-motion features are recognizable by their visual style of doll-like characters with spheroid body parts , and ubiquitous powdery snow using an animation technique called " Animagic " .
(src)="80090"> Often , traditional cel animation scenes of falling snow would be projected over the action to create the effect of a snowfall .
(trg)="147"> ʻO Rankin / Bass Productions , Inc . ( i hoʻokumuʻia e like me Videocraft International , Ltd. a ma hope aku i kapaʻiaʻo Rankin / Bass Animated Entertainment ) he kamupene o ka HuiʻAmelika , iʻikeʻia no kāna mau polokalamu kīwī nui , e like me kāna hana i ka animation animation .
(trg)="148"> Hiki keʻikeʻia nā hiʻohiʻona o ka Rankin / Bass ma ko lākouʻano kiʻikuhi likeʻole me nā pūʻupuʻu spheroid , a me ka hau maeʻa ma ka hoʻohanaʻana i kahiʻenehana hanaʻoni " Animagic " . ʻO ka manawa pinepine , e hoʻolālāʻia nā hanana hula o ka hiona hau i ka hana e hana i ka hopena o ka hau .
(src)="80091"> Nearly all of the studio 's animation was outsourced to at least five Japanese animation companies : MOM Production , Toei Animation , TCJ ( Television Corporation of Japan ) , Mushi Production and Topcraft.[2][3 ]
(trg)="149"> Ma kahi kokoke i nā hanana a pau o ka studio , ua hoʻopukaʻia i nā huiʻoihana Japanese heʻelima : MOM Production , Toei Animation , TCJ ( Television Corporation of Japan ) , Mushi Production andcraftcraft .
(src)="80092"> The company was founded in New York City by Arthur Rankin , Jr. and Jules Bass on September 14 , 1960 , as Videocraft International .
(src)="80093"> The majority of Rankin/Bass ' work , including all of their " Animagic " stop-motion productions ( which they were well known for ) , were created in Tokyo , Japan .
(src)="80094"> Throughout the 1960s , the Animagic productions were headed by Japanese stop-motion animator Tadahito Mochinaga at his studio , MOM Production .
(src)="80095"> He was credited for his supervision as " Tad Mochinaga "
(trg)="150"> Ua hoʻokumuʻia ka hui ma New York City e Arthur Rankin , Jr. a me Jules Bass ma ka lā 14 o Kepakemapa , 1960 , ʻoiaiʻo Worldcraft International . ʻO ka hapanui o ka hana Rankin / Bass , me nā mea hana a pau o ka " Animagic " i hanaʻia ma Tokyo , Iapana .
(trg)="151"> I loko o nā makahiki 1960 , ua alakaʻiʻia nā huahana Animagic e ka mea hoʻokani pila a Tadahito Mochinaga ma kāna keena , MOM Production .
(trg)="152"> Ua kūʻaiʻiaʻo ia no kona nānāʻanaʻo " Tad Mochinaga "

(trg)="502"> Official Website Corporate Website
(src)="80463"> McDonald 's is an American fast food company , founded in 1940 as a restaurant operated by Richard and Maurice McDonald , in San Bernardino , California , United States .
(src)="80464"> They rechristened their business as a hamburger stand , and later turned the company into a franchise , with the Golden Arches logo being introduced in 1953 at a location in Phoenix , Arizona .
(src)="80465"> In 1955 , Ray Kroc , a businessman , joined the company as a franchise agent and proceeded to purchase the chain from the McDonald brothers .
(src)="80466"> McDonald 's had its original headquarters in Oak Brook , Illinois , but moved its global headquarters to Chicago in early 2018.[4][5][6 ]
(trg)="503"> ʻO McDonald kekahi hui meaʻaiʻai wikiwikiʻAmelika , i hoʻokumuʻia i ka makahiki 1940 i kahi hale hoʻokipa e Richard a me Maurice McDonald , ma San Bernardino , Kaleponi , ʻAmelika .
(trg)="504"> Ua hoʻolilo hou lākou i kā lākouʻoihana ma keʻano he hamburger , a ma hope aku ua hoʻololiʻia ka hui , a me ka logo Golden Arches i hoʻokomoʻia i ka makahiki 1953 ma kekahi wahi ma Phoenix , Arizona .
(trg)="505"> I ka makahiki 1955 , ua hoʻokomoʻo Ray Kroc , he mea kālepa , i ka hui ma keʻano he mea kūʻai kālā a kūʻai aku i ke kaulahao mai nā hoahānau McDonald .
(trg)="506"> Ua loaʻa iā McDonald kona keʻena poʻokela ma Oak Brook , Illinois , akā ua hoʻoholoʻo ia i ke keʻena nui o Chicago i ka hoʻomakaʻana o 2018 .
(trg)="507"> [ 4 ] [ 5 ] [ 6 ]
(src)="80467"> McDonald 's is the world 's largest restaurant chain by revenue,[7 ] serving over 69 million customers daily in over 100 countries[8 ] across approximately 36,900 outlets as of 2016.[9 ] Although McDonald 's is known for its hamburgers , they also sell cheeseburgers , chicken products , french fries , breakfast items , soft drinks , milkshakes , wraps , and desserts .
(src)="80468"> In response to changing consumer tastes and a negative backlash because of the unhealthiness of their food,[10 ] the company has added to its menu salads , fish , smoothies , and fruit .
(src)="80469"> The McDonald 's Corporation revenues come from the rent , royalties , and fees paid by the franchisees , as well as sales in company-operated restaurants .
(src)="80470"> According to a BBC report published in 2012 , McDonald 's is the world 's second-largest private employer ( behind Walmart ) with 1.9 million employees , 1.5 million of whom work for franchises .
(trg)="508"> ʻO McDonald ' s ka laikini punahele nui loa o ka honua ma o ka loaʻaʻana , ʻoihana 69 miliona mau kānaka i kēlā me kēia lā ma kahi o 100 mau ' āina ma kahi o 36,900 mau puka ma ka 2016.ʻOiai uaʻikeʻiaʻo McDonald no kona poʻe hamburger , kūʻai lākou i nā pipi , nā mea moa , nā meaʻawaʻawa , nā milkshakes , nāʻaʻahu , a me nā meaʻai .
(trg)="509"> I ka paneʻana i ka loliʻana o nā mea kūʻai mea kūʻai a me ka pale kuʻikuʻi ma muli o ka maikaʻiʻole o kā lākouʻai , ua hoʻohui ka hui i kāna mau meli , iʻa , manuahi , a me nā hua . ʻO ka hōʻai ' ē o McDonald o ka Hui mai loko mai o ka uku , nā uku ' āina , a me nā uku i ukuʻia e nā mea waiwai , a me nā kūʻaiʻana i nā haleʻaina i lawelaweʻia e nāʻoihana .
(trg)="510"> Wahi a kekahi BBC i paʻiʻia i ka makahiki 2012 , ʻo McDonald ' s ka meaʻoihana nui loa o ka honua ( ma hope o Walmart ) me ka 1.9 miliona kānaka , 1.5 miliona o lākou e hana i ka waiwai .
(src)="80478"> Moana ( /moʊˈɑːnə , -ænə/ ) , also known as Vaiana[4 ] or Oceania[5 ] in some markets , is a 2016 American 3D computer-animated musical adventure film produced by Walt Disney Animation Studios and released by Walt Disney Pictures .
(src)="80479"> It is the 56th Disney animated feature film .
(src)="80480"> Directed by Ron Clements and John Musker , co-directed by Don Hall and Chris Williams , the film introduces Auliʻi Cravalho as Moana and features the voices of Dwayne Johnson , Rachel House , Temuera Morrison , Jemaine Clement , Nicole Scherzinger , and Alan Tudyk .
(src)="80481"> The film features songs written by Lin-Manuel Miranda and Opetaia Foa'i and orchestral score composed by Mark Mancina .
(trg)="511"> Moana o ka 2016 ' Amelika 3D kamepiula-Animated bila hoike ia ho film hua mai la ia e Walt Disney ka pāpaho o Nuioka ma a hoʻokuʻuʻia e nā Walt Disney Nā kiʻi .
(trg)="512"> Hōʻikeʻia kēia kiʻiʻo Auliʻi Cravalho i Moana .
(src)="80486"> Auliʻi Cravalho ( /aʊˈliːʔi krəˈvɑːljoʊ/ ; [ 2][3 ] born November 22 , 2000)[1 ] is an American actress and singer who made her acting debut as the title character in the 2016 film Moana.[4][5][6][7 ] In 2018 , Cravalho made her television debut starring as Lilette Suarez in the NBC drama series Rise .
(trg)="513"> Auli ' ii Cravalho ( hanau November 22 , 2000 ) mea he Amelika mea hana keaka a me ka hoolea i i kona hanaʻiʻo akula nō Debut like ke poʻo inoa i ka Moana 2016ʻo Moana .

(src)="80490"> Pratibhasthali is a girls school started by Acharya Vidyasagar .
(src)="80491"> Schools are operational in Jabalpur , Dongargarh , Ramtek , Paporaji and Indore in India.[1][2 ]
(trg)="517"> ʻO Pratibhasthali kahi kula kamaliʻi i hoʻomakaʻia e Acharya Vidyasagar .
(trg)="518"> Ke holo nei nā kula ma Jabalpur , Dongargarh , Ramtek , Paporaji , a me Indore ma India . [ 1 ] [ 2 ]
